Note: This file is a committed review snapshot. Generated `qa-output/` bundles remain uncommitted. Some very large Study Panel arrays are represented by the QA harness review sample size; Source Discovery and Reference Graph are included at the current full Matthew 1 count because their QA sample limit covers all current records.
